
*******************************************
Cold Princess

*******************************************
 A/N: Dedicated to Ms. Filipina. I was inspired by her story, IDTIP. ^^V 

****

 

PROLOGUE: 

 

 


"Bitch, move."

 

"Huh?"

 

"Are you deaf? MOVE!"

 

 

 

The bitch stood up and move. She should be scared of me. Everybody should. Once I say a word, people should obey me. I'm great, powerful. Bitcher than all the bitches.

Every eye on the cafe was on me, watching every move I make. They're giving it to me, the thing I want. ATTENTION.

 


I'm cold. The way I speak, the way I act. Every move I make is cold. You can defy me a cold-hearted gal who haves fun when using a bitch as a punching bag, not reminding myself that it's a person. I love to fight. All I do is fight, jam, drink, have fun. I don't have friends. I once had, but she turned me down. That was years ago, when I was weak.

 

Yes, there's a reason behind this cold mask of mine. A reason that changed me. I thought being kind all the time will give me great and true people around me, but it was just a hunch.


See, I changed I alot. Thanks to those bitches and assholes that made fun of me, that looked down at me. Now, I'll make them feel the sweet taste of revenge. The what-you-so-called weak nerd came back. Not as the old one, but as the new one. The Cold Princess.

One //

*******************************************
 A/N: Natats ako sa mga comment niyo sa Prologue, so here it is! :))) THANK YOU PO ULIT!! ^^VV

NERD na Charlotte on the side -->


*****

 

Point of View

-Charlotte Dy-

 

 

 

3 years ago..

 

 

"Hahaha! Nerd ka na nga, lampa ka pa!"


Laughter filled the canteen. Lahat sila, pinagtatawanan ako. Naglalakad ako hawak ang isang cup ng hot chocolate nang patirin ako ng sikat na bratinella ng school, si Hannah. She's the class president, SSG governor, the owner of the school I study in. Everyone praise her. Kapag dadaan siya, lahat tatabi. Takot sila makaaway si Hannah.

Tumayo ako, punong-puno ng kahihiyan. Tumakbo ako papunta sa comfort room. Buti nalang walang tao, ako lang.

 

"Haaaay, Charlotte. Hanggang kelan ka magpapa-api kay Hannah? Alam ko kaya mo siya, di mo lang magawa.." kinakausap ko sarili ko sa harap ng salamin. Tinignan ko ang sarili ko, ang dumi na ng damit ko dahil sa hot chocolate na tumapon saken. Bigla nalang akong naiyak. Hindi ko na kaya ang pambubully nila saken, sobra na sila..

 

"Kung gusto mo, I'll help you. Don't cry and act stupid for the rest of your life." Nagulat ako ng biglang may lumabas sa isa sa mga cubicle. Si Rachel, best friend ni Hannah. Pumunta siya sa harap ng salamin, sa tabi ko. She smiled. "I'll help you get your revenge, if you want."

 

"Re-revenge?"

 


"Yeah. As you said, to yourself, kaya mo si Hannah pero di mo lang magawa. I'll help you with that." Nagaayos siya ng lipstick niya at tumingin sakin. Pinagmamasdan ko siya, alam kong best friend niya si Hannah. Tumalikod siya sa salamin at humarap sakin. "I know nagdadalawang isip because I'm Hannah's best friend. But my dear, I grew tired of her games. I want a new friend. And I guess, you need a friend. So... Friends?" Inabot niya sakin ung kanang kamay niya. Hindi ko alam kung aabutin ko ba un o hindi. Pero, napagisip ko rin na ngayon palang ako magkakaroon ng kaibigan dito sa school mula ng lumipat ako a year ago.

 

"Friends." Ngumiti ako sa kanya. Who knows, siguro nga, kelangan din niya ng kaibigan.

 

"Yey!" niyakap niya ako. Pero bigla siyang napabitaw, naalala ko, basa nga pala yung damit ko. "Uhh, Charlotte. I have extra shirt in my locker, use that. You're effin' wet." Lumabas kami sa comfort room at dumiretso sa locker room. Binigay sakin ni Rachel ung shirt niya then sinamahan niya ako pabalik sa comfort room.

 

Since then, lagi na kame magkasama ni Rachel. Ngayon ko lang naramdaman ang magkaroon ng kaibigan. Yung may kasama ka kumain sa canteen kapag break time, may ka-partner ka sa activity sa isang subject, yung may kakwentuhan ka habang may pinapagalitan ung teacher niyo. Di ko akalain na magkakaroon pa ko ng kaibigan.

 

Until one day, may kumakalat na balita na ginagamit lang daw ako ni Rachel para tumaas ang grades niya. Nung una, hindi ko yun pinaniwalaan, pero nung sinabi ni Hannah ang lahat ng nalalaman niya, tsaka ko lang naisip na totoo nga. Kinausap ko si Rachel noon,

 

 

"Bakit mo nagawa yun Rachel? Akala ko, magkaibigan tayo?"

"Tsh. Ginawa ko lang yun, 'cause Hannah asked me to. Hindi naman talaga ako willing na maging friend ka noh. I never wanted a nerd friend. *grin*"

"P-pero, Rachel." umiiyak ako. hindi ko aakalain na lolokohin lang ako ng nagiisa kong kaibigan. "Ang sama, sama mo! Sabi mo sakin ayaw mo na kay Hannah, kaya ginawa mo akong friend mo!"

 

Tumayo siya sa kinauupuan niya, "My dear, haven't you heard of the rumors? I just used you to gain, let's just say, intelligence, to get good grades. As I have said, I never wanted a nerd friend." She grinned.

 

 

****

 

 

"Charlotte, anak. Are you ready? Aalis na tayo maya-maya. Your Dad is waiting for us."

 

"Yes, mom.."

 

 

Asa airport kame ngayon. Papunta ng States. At first, si Mom lang ang aalis, but because sa mga nangyare sakin, I asked her if I can come. She willingly agreed.

Napagdesisyunan ko na umalis para magbago, to be a new Charlotte. Magaaral ako sa States, babaguhin ko sarili ko. Hindi ko na hahayaan na maapi pa ulit ako, na maloko ulet. Babalik ako, kapag ayos na ang lahat. Kapag hindi na ako yung nerd na palaging binu-bully, yung nerd na laging inuutusan, yung nerd na mahina. I'll be back. At sisigurudahin kong pagbalik ko, hindi na ako ung dating Charlotte. Sisiguraduhin kong ang Charlotte na babalik ay yung malakas, walang inaatrasan.

Two //

*******************************************
 

 

Point of View

-Charlotte Dy-

 

 

3 years passed. The moments when I'm being bullied flashed back in my mind. I still remember those days, and I will never ever forget those. Especaially the people who thought me how to be strong, the people that bullied me.

 

 

"Hey! I got this first!" there she is.

"I don't care! I saw this first, so hand it over." Ms. Oh-so-zombie-fac

"No! This is mine!"

 

Ugh. They're so irritating! -_______-

 

"Hand it to her, bitch." i said coldly to Ms. Oh-so-zombie-face

"Who are you? And how dare you call me bitch!"

"If you don't give that to her, you're a fvckng bitch. Will 'ya?" Ms. Oh-so-zombie-face handed the dress to her. I can see that her face is turning red because of anger. Psh. Serves her right -____-

 

"And you." I looked at Natasha. "Pay that, now."

 

I just glared at her. That's Natasha Atkinson, my British friend. You heard it right. I thought I would never get a friend. But she's so childish. It almost took her 3 months just so we can be friends. The day we became friends was when she climbed up my window just to give pizzas 'cause it's her birthday. I found it crazy, but it shows how true she is to me.


I waited for her until she paid that fvckng dress. She's so damn shoppaholic. She almost spent 4 hours buying this and that. She buys everything she see. Ugh. While here I am, following her. I can't leave her alone shopping. She's been good to me the past years so let me be good to her. She's my friend. Best friend.

 

"Natasha, can we go home now?" I asked her with my cold voice.

"Nah. Let's eat first. Ice cream? My treat!" She smiled. She knows what my weakness is -___-

"That's why you're getting fat. Ugh. Hurry up."

 

We entered the ice cream parlor that have my favorite flavor of ice cream. Natasha ordered for me while I find our seats. I found one beside the window. The chairs are comfortable, so it's fine with me. Natasha arrived at the table with my ice cream. She sat infront of me. I took the spoon and eat like I didn't eat for a month.

 

"Hey, slowly, Charlotte. You're gonna have indigestion." Natasha said.

"Natasha, this is ice cream. It melts in my mouth, I can't have indigestion with this." 
I said to her as I entered the spoon full of ice cream on my mouth.

"Alright, alright. But.. Are you really moving back to the Philippines? I mean, you're leaving me here? ALONE?!" she shouted.

 

"Don't shout. You can come if you like." 

"Really, I can?! I would love to! When is your flight?" Now sheshouted with happiness. Oh god. She's so bipolar!

"Psh. You only like to come with me because you want to go to the malls and buy all their stuff." the ice cream melted in my mouth. Ugh, this will be the last time I'll eat this ice cream.

 

"Well, you're right 'bout that. But aside from that, I want to be with you! You know I'm all alone with myself.." she flashed a sad face.

 

Natasha lived by all herself for 2 years. Her parents died on a car accident. I was her only friend by that time. So, I became a sister to her, just so she wouldn't be sad. "Drop the topic, Natasha. Don't bring it up, you'll just cry again and I'll have to comfort you. Just eat your ice cream, so I can prepare my things. Tomorrow is my flight." I said coldly. I don't want her to be sad again so I allowed her to come with me in the Philippines.

 

She smiled weakly, "Thanks, Charlotte. I owe you big time." she ate her ice cream.

 

I looked at her. She's just a silly girl who doesn't have any friends aside from me. She only have me.And i'd be willing to be with her forever. Though my attittude is not like hers: jolly, loud, crazy, talkative and shoppalic -- I still appreciate her. It's not just me who needs a friend, she also needs one. And I'm here for her.

 

I drove back to my condominium after dropping Natasha to her house. I already packed some of my things last night, but I still have some to pack. Tomorrow, is the start. The start of something new. I'm coming back, the nerd is gonna come back. But not with a face of a nerd. But with a face of a cold bitch that was humiliated.

Three //

*******************************************
 

 

Point of View

-Charlotte Dy-

 

 

 

 

"Omo! Is this a palace?" Natasha said as soon as we entered my house.

 

Yeah, right. MY house. Mommy built this for me, so I can have a cool place where I can stay while here in the Philippines. Ugh! I missed it here..

 

"Welcome home po, Ma'am." Pagbati samin ni Nanay Rosa.

"Nay Rosa, I told you not to call me Ma'am. Charlotte will do, ok?"

"I'm sorry, Ma'-- Charlotte. Hindi na kasi ako sanay. 3 years ka ring wala dito.." Si Nay Rosa yung caretaker netong bahay ko. Tumatayo na rin bilang second Mom ko. Sa kanya ko pinagkatiwala 'to for 3 years. 3 years, since Mom died.

 

"Nay Rosa, by the way. This is Natasha, my friend. Friend ko sa States." Pinakilala ko si Natasha ka Nay Rosa. Ngumiti naman si Nay Rosa.

 

"Ay, anak. Ako nga pala si Nanay Rosa." Natasha looked puzzled. I smirked.

 

"Nay Rosa, di po siya nakakaintindi ng tagalog. Englishera po yan, nosebleed." I turned to Nay Rosa.

 

"Ay ganun ba? Nako, iha! Magaling yata ako mag english!" Kinindatan ako ni Nay Rosa, then she looked at Natasha. "Hello, I'm Nay Rosa. I'm Charlotte's second Mom, and also the caretaker of this house." Nay Rosa smiled to Natasha. Same as Natasha to Nay Rosa.

 

I think magkakasundo naman din sila Nay Rosa at Natasha. Mabait si Nay Rosa. Mommy hired her as my personal yaya before kame pumunta ng States. Pero dahil pinagawa ni Mommy 'tong mansion ko, nagpaiwan nalang si Nay Rosa para bantayan 'tong bahay ko. Sobrang bait talaga niyan ni Nay Rosa..

Mukha namang nagkakasundo na nga sila. Pupunta muna ako kay Mommy..

 

"Nay Rosa, samahan niyo nalang po si Natasha sa kwarto niya. Dun nalang po siya sa kwarto katabi nung aken." I turned to Natasha. "Natasha, I'll just go somewhere. Suit yourself here."

"I will. Mind if you tell me where you're going?" Psh. Pakilamera din 'tong babaeng 'to eh. Kung di lang siya best friend ko --__________-

"I'm going to my Mom.." I grabbed the keys to my big bike. It's been years since I last rode my big bike. I missed the sound of it when I opened the engine.

 

Sinuot ko na yung helmet ko and umalis. Mabilis ako magpatakbo ng mga ganto. When I was in States, lagi akong nakikipag car racing. Kung di car racing, motor race. And to tell you the truth, I'm the best at those. No one can beat me. Even those goddamn bastards who doesn't do anything but to talk and talk. Saying that they're great at that, no truthfully, they're not.

Nandito na ko. Nandito na ko Mommy.. Sa puntod niya..

 

Pinarada ko yung big bike ko sa tapat ng puntod ni Mommy, nilagay ko ung helmet dun. I can't wait na makausap si Mommy.

 

Umupo ako sa tapat puntod niya..

 

"Mommy, how have you been? It's been 3 years.. I miss you.. alot." Before I notice, tears are falling from my eyes. "Mom, nandito na po ulit ako. Nakauwi na ko galing States. Sinama ko po si Natasha. Mom, kilala niyo po si Natasha di ba? Siya lang yung friend na tumagal saken. Kaya, grateful ako." Pag andito ako kay Mommy, nawawala yung pagka-cold ko. Lumalabas yung dating ako. Yung weak. "Mommy.. Alam niyo po ba? Simula nung nawala kayo, I changed. Ang laki ng pinagbago ko.. Naging rebelde ako, car racing every night. I always fight. Sumama pa nga ako sa isang gang sa States eh. Sometimes, I'm in the bar, drinking. Dancing my heart out. I don't know Mom.. Malungkot ang buhay ko since nawala ka sa tabi ko. Si Natasha, naging sister ko siya. Mommy, alam mo ba? Parehas kami ni Natasha. Wala na din siyang parents. Mommy, alam niyo po ba? Sabi sakin ni Dad bago kame pumunta dito sa Pilipinas, ako daw yung Heiress ng Mafia niya. Mommmy, okay lang po ba? Kasi.. Alam ko po, ayaw niyo ako sumali sa ganun eh. Pero, Mommy.. Gusto ko po. Ugh. Bahala nalang po Mommy.. Oo nga po pala, naisip ko po na pumasok sa JDU. Mommy, sayang di ikaw yung principal dun ngayon. Sana Mommy, ikaw parin. Mommy, I miss you na.." Napahagulgol ako. Ngayon nalang ulet ako umiyak ng ganto. "Super I miss you, Mommy. Sana andito ka nalang.."Before I knew, it was raining. "Mommy, una na po ako. Umuulan na po eh. Babalik po ako. Bye, Mommy.." 

 

Tumayo na ko. For the last time, tinignan ko yung puntod ni Mommy. Bumalik na ko sa big bike ko at sinuot yung helmet.

 

"Shit! Basa! Ugh. Right. -________-" Bumabalik na yung pagiging cold ko. Basa yung big bike ko, lalo pang lumakas yung ulan. Pinaandar ko na yun at pinakatakbo ng mabilis. In 5 minutes, nakauwi na ko.

 

"Oh my God Charlotte! You're freaking wet!" Sinalubong ako ni Natasha ng sigaw. Nanonood siya ng movie sa living room. Ugh. Di ko nalang siya pinansin at nagtuloy-tuloy sa room ko.

 

Naligo ako. Then humiga sa kama ko. Pinikit ko mga mata ko. My head hurts.

 

Naalala ko 3 years ago. Si Hannah at Rachel. Babawian ko pa sila, I'll have my revenge. Mageenroll ako sa school bukas. I told Mommy. Tatapusin ko pag aaral ko. 4th year college na rin naman ako. And if mageenroll ako, middle of the semester na. Ok lang. Advance naman yung turo sa States, I can catch up with that.

Hannah and Rachel, I still remember the humiliation that you gave to my pride.

 

 

 

It's payback time.

Point of View

-Natasha Atkinson-

 

 

 

Hey there! Did Charlotte introduced me to you guys? Well, if yes. GREAT! If not, but I think she already introduced me, I'll still introduce myself..

 

I'm Natasha Collie Atkinson. Everybody calls me Natasha. Supposedly they do, because Charlotte is the only friend I have. Even Charlotte simply calls me 'Natasha', but sometimes 'Ash'. It's cool, anyway. I'm 18 years old, born in England. I accompanied Charlotte here in the Philippines 'cause I know she doesn't have any friends here. She once told me that she used to have one friend when she was in high school. But that friend of hers betrayed her, as Charlotte said.

 

Charlotte had been my best friend. She's always there for me when I'm in trouble. Like what happened in the mall before we fled to the Philippines. She was like my Princess-in-shining-armor. Yeah, 'Princess'. She's a girl. >:) But aside from being my best friend, she also treats me as her OWN sister. Yes, she's cold. Everything she do is frightening. But I did whatever I can do so that she can be my friend. When we was in States, they we're newly moved in to the house next to mine. She was so quiet. When I look at her, it always give me the creeps. She's scary when she looks at you. I know that she needs a friend to lean on. I see her everyday by herself. I approached her and asked if we could be friends. She refused. But I didn't lose hope. I still irritate her. But later on, we became friends because of a pizza. Hahaha. Weird right?

 

I tell you guys, Charlotte is not that bad. She's just cold. She maybe fierce, heartless and scary on the outside. But deep inside, she's so nice and caring. She understands people around her. She never lets anyone beaten up, though sometimes she beats someone. She only beat someone for some reason. She may not tell it and hide it all to herself. But, believe me, she always have a reason.

 

By the way, today we'll go to JD University. It's a school, OBVIOUSLY. Charlotte said she wants to continue her studies. But she's already in 4th year college, why bother study if she have her mother's bussiness? Not my problem. But, the thing is..

 

"Charlotte! I have I favor to ask.." I shouted to her. She was at her room. I was outside.

"What is it?!" Though she yellled, there's still coldness in her voice.

"Can you also enroll me to that University?!"

"...." she didn't answered.

 

It's been minutes since she didn't answered. I stood frozen outside her room, my ears stuck to the door. Listening what's she doing inside..

 

"OUCH!"

"Tsk. Natasha, stalker much?" Her voice is soooo cold. She helped me stand up.

"Sorry. Anyway, about what I asked earlier.. Can you also enroll me to that Uni---" Bad girl. I'm talking then she suddenly puts her finger on my lips.

"Why would I ask you to come if I'm not enrolling you?" She crossed her arms. Oh god! I told you guys, SHE'S NICE!

"Really? I can also? Wooow. Thanks, Charlotte!" She walked past me.

"C'mon. Hurry up." I followed her up to the garage. Wow, this girl is really rich. Imagine, she have 8 cars and 2 big bikes in her garage. And her house is goddamn big. Ohnonono, her palace.

"Natasha, we're here."

"I met my destiny...." I said to her. But she just looked at me with disgust. Right, Charlotte's a man-hater. -____- She walked past me, I just followed her.

 

Now, I'm walking like an idiot. This smile can't get out of my lips. Oh.. How I really wish that we can meet again. I guess, I found my destiny..

We're still young, maybe 4 years old nung nakilala ko si Charlotte. She was crying alone at the park. I offered her ice cream so she would stop crying. She accepted it and we became friends. Since then she was my friend. And the thing is.. I loved her since that day.

 

Naghiwalay kame noon dahil kelangan ko pumunta sa Korea. 11 years akong nandon. 11 years na nangungulila kay Charlotte. She was my first love.

 

Kaya noong bumalik ako sa Pilipinas, the first thing I did was to find her. And luckily I did. Pumasok ako sa pinapasukan niyang school. Tinarayan pa nga niya ako nung una. Hindi na niya ako nakilala. Siguro.. kinalimutan na niya yung kababata niya..

 

 

"Sir, sisimulan na po namin.." 

 

 

Tinurukan ako ng amnestesia ng doctor. This is it.

 

 

Charlotte Dy. I love you and I'm willing to give my life for you..

Point of View

-Natasha Atkinson-

 

 

From: Nathan <3

Let's meet later, I have something to tell you. ;-)

 

Isn't that exciting?! Seriously guys, me and Nathan have something already. It's not that we're already a couple. You know, getting-to-know-each-other. And I'm sooooooooooooo SAD 'cause we're still there. I mean, it's been.. months, I think, since we've met each other. I told him that I like him, he was... I don't know. But the other time, he also told me that he like me. That time, I almost collapsed. Swear to death.

 

I'm still here at Char's room. Think of that girl, she has two suitors yet she doesn't care? Having two suitors is my dream. But since I found Nathan, I think that dream is nothing no more. I already found a guy that I'll love forever and ever. As the teleserye say, "Walang Hanggan" or Infinite.

 

Alright, I suck at tagalog. I should learn how to speak some. It's not nice speaking English in a British way here in Philippines. I'm on the Philippines, not in UK.

 

I asked Char a while ago if we can go to the mall, she said yes the first time. But when her suitors came, she just left me alone. Oh well, It's great if it's just the two of us, Nathan and me, walking.. talking. Sounds great!

 

I got up and went to my room. Charlotte already left. That girl, I hope she chooses the one that her heart shouts for. On my opinion, I like Francis more than Yun Ju. But, Yun Ju's sweeter than Francis. Anyway, let's not get involved in their "love story". Let's get going on MY love story. Ok, ok. Whatever for me. Hahaha.

 

I took at bath and wore something nice. Sicne I don't know how to drive I just took a cab going to the mall. It's so confusing why'd we met at the mall, of all places. But, isn't it sweet? Ok, too much for the blushing.

 

Nathan texted me to meet at the Starbucks. While I walk, everyone was, like, looking or staring. Wonder why.. Before I took a seat, I ordered something, ofcourse. I forgot to eat lunch.

 

Nathan is almost, I think, an hour late. I keep texting him, but he's not texting back. Tried calling him, he's not picking up. I finished my food, he's not yet around. I look like a poor girl waiting for her daddy. I'm starting to get pissed!

 

"Excuse me, you're Natasha, right? Natasha Atkinson?" A guy that looks like Nathan, but absolutely NOT Nathan, approached me. Should I answer him? Char told me to don't talk to someone I don't know.

 

I just smiled at him. It's rude if I don't answer him. But I remembered what Char said so I just smiled at him. He took his phone from his pocket and called someone.

 

"Ne, hyung. Andito siya.. Eh?! Baka mapagkamalan pa kong kidnapper!... Alright, give me your credit card later as payment, arasso?... Hahaha, osige. San nga ulet?...  Ah, ok! Annyeong~" 

 

Ow--kay. He's speaking 3 languages. Tagalog, English and Korean. I envy him. I swear, I do. I'm dying to speak Tagalog. -_________- He returned his phone on his jeans' pocket and turned to me.

 

"Excuse me, mind if I take you somewhere?" 

 

I didn't answer back. He's words are creepy but his face isn't.

 

"Oh! Don't worry, I won't do something bad to you. I'd be killed, if so. So, let's go?" 

 

He's kinda nice. And looks nice. Maybe I should trust him. Alright, I got up from my seat. I followed him up to the rooftop. As soon as I entered the place, it was so dark. It's almost 8pm. The guy I was following was nowhere to be found. Where the heck is he? -_________-

 

I keep on walking. I stopped for awhile. I really can't see a thing. Ugh. Then moments later, the lights suddenly opened.

 

The whole place was fantastic! Rose petals everywhere. Music's starting to play. A mini stage at the end, where there are 3 guys singing. I saw the guy that accompanied me through here. I'm starting to get amazed of the place. What is this place?

 

"You liked it?" 

 

I heard a voice coming from behind me. I turned around and there I saw him.

 

"Nathan.."

"I'm sorry for being late. I was preparing this."

 

He looked around the place, me too. I looked at him, again. Tears began to fall from my eyes. I don't know why or how..

 

"Hey, stop crying. Didn't you liked it?" His voice was worried. He came near me then wiped those tears.

"I liked it.. Really do.." My voice was trembling. Maybe because I'm crying.

 

Nathan chuckled.He hugged me. I can feel my heart beating.. I can feel the time moving slow, thinking we're the only ones here in this place. It feels like time stopped.

 

He removed his arms wrapped around me, faced me then smiled. Please don't do that, I'm melting..

 

"Dance with me?" He offered his hand then he led me to the mini stage. Slow music started to play and the lights were dim. We stopped at the center then he held my waist. I wrapped my arms around his neck. We're dancing slow..

 

"I love you.." He whispered in my ear. Again, I can feel my tears running down on my cheeks. Those words were sweet.. I hugged him, but we're still slow dancing.

 

How I waited for a moment like this. It was like a fairytale. A magical tale that I'd never thought It would happen in real life. But it did. And it happened to me. Being loved by the one you like is like buying your favorite thing in it's lowest price. Love can do everything. Love is magic.

 

"I love you, too.." I faced him. We stared on each others eyes for a moment then magic happened.

 

I wanted to feel this magic. I thought I would just feel this when I get married. But I think I'm wrong. This magic was so great. We're kissing passionately.

 

If this is a dream, while I hope it's not, I wish it wouldn't end. I wish it would last longer. And I hope I woundn't wake up anymore.

 

Love conquers all. Even the simplest person on Earth can fall inlove. No one is exempted for love. Once you've been hit, you can't do nothing at all but to love him back. 'Cause it's magic that puts you together.

 

The guy infront of me is love. The thing between us.. is magic.

"Si Yun Ju? Ano nangyare sa kanya?"

"Long story. So, ang pinagtataka ko lang. Bakit galit si Francis sayo?"  

 

  
Kinwento ko kay Charlotte yung lahat ng nangyare 2 years ago. Na pinagbantaan yung buhay ni Francis kaya ayun.

And Third, natatakot ako sa magiging sagot niya. Ayokong marinig na hindi na niya ako mahal sa bibig niya. Alam ko, hindi na nga niya ako mahal. Pero, sobrang sakit pag sinabi niya sakin yun.

 Pagkasabi niya nun. Umalis na siya. Anong ibig sabihin naman ni Char dun?  

 

Nung nakapagisip-isip nako, umalis na din ako dun. Ano bang gagawin ko?! I still love Francis. I don't know how to face him. Pag kinausap ko siya, for sure, magiging cold lang siya sakin. Hindi papansinin, swerte ko nalang kung pansinin ako nun. Kapag nainis naman ako sa sagot niya, sisigawan ko siya. Tapos sigawan na kame. Walang magandang patutunguhan yung ganun namin eh. -___________-    

 

Aish. Uuwi nalang ako.      

 

 

Alam ko, dadating din yung oras para makapagusap kame ni Francis.

May nakita akong shooting star.

 

Pinikit ko yung mga mata ko at humiling..

Binuksan ko muli yung mga mata ko. Nakita kong si Francis na nakapikit. Nagulat naman ako ng buksan niya ung mga yun. Napatingin ulit ako sa langit. Nakakahiya >_________<

Tsaka ko lang nalaman..

 

 

We're still looking at the same star.

"Huh? Ah. Wala. :)" 

"Nakakagulat na makita kitang nakangiti, anak. I think, this is the first time I ever saw you.. smile?" Dahil kay Taeyang.

"Wala yun, Dad." Yung boses ko, bumalik sa pagiging cold. "Ba't niyo nga pala ako hinanap?"

"Ano yun?" Ang seryoso ng boses ni Dad oh. Ano kaya yun?

States? Tumayo si Dad tas may kinuha sa desk niya. May binigay siya sakin. Plane ticket.

Naisip ko si Yun Ju. Babalik ako sa States? Siguro nga.. It's better off that way, right?

 

Tumango nalang ako kay Dad. "I'll think about that. Matagal pa naman expiration netong ticket." Tumayo ako, "Sige Dad. Matutulog nako." 

 

Niyakap ko muna si Dad tapos lumabas na sa office niya at pumunta sa kwarto ko. Humiga ako sa kama. Tinignan yung ticket.

 

Parang.. gusto kong umalis. Na hindi.

 Yun Ju honeybunch 
calling...

I'm going back to States.

"D-dad?"

Dahil sa hindi ako makapaniwala, lumapit ako sa kama ni Charlotte. At totoo nga ang hinala ko. Gising na siya. Gising na siya!

 

 

Nagsilapitan naman sila Gail, Taeyang, Francis at Aphrodite sa kama. Nakapalibot kameng lahat. Masaya. Masaya kase nagising na ang taong dahilan kung baket kame nandito ngayon.

 

 

"Dad..?" Inayos ni Tito Edward sa pagkakahiga si Charlotte para makaupo siya ng mabuti. Nung nakaupo na siya, tsaka naman siya kinausap ni Tito Edward.

 

"Anak, Charlotte? Ayos ka na ba?" 

"D-dad.. I'm fine."

"Sigurado ka? Walang masakit sayo?" 





"Tss. Dad, ang kulit mo. ~~." 


 

 

Natuwa ako sa sinabi niya. Hindi lang nagising si Charlotte Dy. Gising na gising na siya. Dahil ayan na yung pagkacold niya.

 

 

"Hi, pusa ko!" -Francis.

"Francis? Andito ka?" -Charlotte.

"Hindi, pusa ko. Picture ko lang 'to. Nabulag ka na ba?" 

"Ah, picture ka lang pala. K." -Charlotte. Hindi lang siya cold. Masunget pa. -______-

"Pusa ko naman eh!" Parang bata si Francis.

 

"Hahaha! Joke lang!" Tama ba nakita't narinig ko? Tumawa si Charlotte?

"Pusa ko talaga. Tss. Tignan mo nga oh," tinaas niya yung kamay niyang hawak yung kamay ni Aphrodite. "Sinunod ko yung sinabi mo nun! Kame na ni Aphrodite ^_____________^" 

Nagblush naman si Aphrodite, "He he. Kaw talaga, Francis. Kahiya." Tumingin siya kay Charlotte. "Hehe, haha. Hi, Char~" 

 

"Seriously? Kayo na? Hahaha!" Kanina pa tawa ng tawa 'tong si honeybunch ah? Pero ang sarap pakinggan ng tawa niya. ^___________^

 

 

"Hi, Charlotte~ ^_________^" -Gail. Ngumiti naman si Charlotte nung nakita si Gail.

"Gail! Awww-- Hehe. Musta na?" Bakit ang hyper ni honeybunch? XD




"Eto ayos lang naman. Alam mo ba na etong si Yun Ju atat na atat na gumising ka na?" Tinuro niya ako. Napatingin naman si honeybunch saken tapos ngumiti. Tapos balik tingin kay Gail. "Hahaha! Buti naman nagising ka na! Uy! Bonding tayo paglabas mo dito ah?" 

"Hahaha. Sige ba!" -Charlotte.

 

 

"Annyeong, Charlotte. :)" -Pandak.

"Taeyang! Andito ka ren?" -Charlotte.

 

"Yep. How are you? :)" 

"I'm fine. How 'bout you? Hahaha!"

"Happy. Finally you woke up. :)"

"Talaga? Kaw ah! Hahaha" 

 

 

Ang hyper lang talaga ni Charlotte. Seryoso. Hindi naman siya tawa ng tawa lage dati bago siya masagasaan diba? Baket ngayon.. Tawa na siya ng tawa? Ang cute lang niya ^____________^

 

 

"Oo nga pala anak, si Yun Ju---" 

 

"Dad, ano nangyare saken?" Bigla namang naging seryoso yung mukha niya.

"Ah, ano. Nasagasaan ka kase. Don't you remember?" Nagtataka naman yung tanong ni Tito Edward.

"Hmmmm.. All I remember is that I was talking to Gail at the park. That's all." 

 

"Don't you remember crossing the road?" -Gail.

"No, not at all." 

 

"Ganun? Dahil siguro nabagok ulo mo. By the way, si Yun Ju oh!" -Gail. Ngumiti ako kay Honeybunch tapos ngumiti din siya saken. Shit. How I missed her smile!

 

"Hello!" Ngumiti siya. Lumapit ako sa kanya. Sa gilid niya. Sila Tito Edward, Francis at Aphordite naupo na dun sa maliit na kama sa gilid. Kameng tatlo -- Ako, Gail at Taeyang -- nalang nandito sa paligid ni honeybunch.


"Honeybunch! I missed you!" Niyakap ko siya. Syempre hindi muna mahigpit kase baka masaktan pa siya.

 

"I.. missed you.. too? :)" Ang cute talaga ng ngiti ni honeybunch!

 

"Sigurado ka bang wala ng masakit sayo? Ha?" Hinawakan ko magkabilang braso niya.

"Yep, pretty sure! :)" 

 

Napangiti ako. Kahit na medyo naninibago ako kay honeybunch sa pag ngiti ngiti niya, masaya parin ako kase palangiti na siya unlike dati ^______^

 

Napansin ko yung nakasuot sa leeg niya. Kapareha ng necklace na suot ko. Yung necklace na regalo niya sakin nung birthday ko. Couple necklace pala yun? Hindi ko na tatanggalin yung sa leeg ko magpakailanman! ^________________________________^

 

 

"Honeybunch, date tayo? :)" 

Ngumiti siya. "Err.. Hehe. :) Wait. Do I know you?"

 

 

Napatigil ako sa sinabi niya. Shit. Hindi niya ako nakikilala? Kita ko naman yung ekspresyon ng mukha ni Gail, gulat.

 

 

"Honeybunch? Di mo ko kilala? Ako 'to. Si Yun Ju. Honeybunch mo." Pageexplain ko sa kanya. Nakangiti pa rin siya. Pero naguguluhan.

 

"I'm sorry. Are you a friend?" Napatulala na talaga ako sa sinabi ni honeybunch. Shit naman!

 

Lumapit na samin si Tito Edward. Si Gail lumabas para tumawag ng doctor. Shit. Am I hearing this right?!

 

"Anak? You don't remember Yun Ju? He's your boyfriend." -Tito Edward.

 

 

Tumingin ako kay Charlotte. Nagaantay ng isasagot niya. Finally, "Hindi talaga, Dad. Is he someone you know? Pero.. boyfriend? Dad, I don't remember I have a boyfriend." Nakangiti pa rin siya the whole time na sinabi niya yang mga yan.

 

Shit lang! Ano ba 'to?! BAKET HINDI AKO MAALALA NI HONEYBUNCH?!

 

Dumating na si Gail kasama yung doctor. Tinanong ni Tito Edward kung baket hindi ako maalala ni Charlotte tapos sila naalala naman niya. Ako, tulala pa rin. Hindi makapagsalita. Gulat.

 

 

"Maybe she's suffering from what they call Retrograde amnesia. Kapag may gantong amnesia ang isang tao, she may forget the things happened in the past. Pero maaalala din niya yun." Sabi ni Doc.

"Pero, doc. Baket si Yun Ju lang ang hindi niya maalala?" -Gail

 

"Dahil siguro, noong bago pa man magkaroon ng amnesia ang pasyente, he is the one last seen by the patient. Or maybe.. This guy buried alot of memories to the patient na naging dahilan ng hindi niya pagkakaalala dito." -Doc

 

"Doc, that doesn't makes sense!" Nagkaroon ako ng lakas na makapagsalita. Nagulat silang lahat sa pagsigaw ko.

 

 

Lumapit si Gail sakin, pinapakalma ako. How can I calm down?!

 

Tumingin ulit ako kay Charlotte.

 

 

 

"Honeybunch. Hindi mo ba talaga ako naaalala?" 

 

 

My voice was desperate. I was holding her hand. Nakatingin sa kanya. Nakatingin din siya saken. Hindi ko na alam ang gagawin ko kung negative ang sagot ni Charlotte.

 

 

 

 

 

 

"I'm sorry. I really don't know you."

*******************************************
Epilogue

*******************************************
 

 

REMINDER. POV ni KIM YUN JU ang epilogue.

-*-

 

EPILOGUE:

 

 


Her eyes. Her smile. The way she laugh. The way she talks to me.

 

 

Akala ko, happy ending ang saamin ni honeybunch.

 

Pero hindi pala.

 

 

Marami talagang pagsubok ang dumadating sa buhay natin.

 

But this one, kakaiba. 

 

 

I wasn't expecting this.

 

Gusto ko lang, masaya kame ni honeybunch.

 

Gusto ko lang, happy ending para saamin.

 

 

Amnesia.

 

Dahil jan, nawala lahat.

 

Naalala niya ang lahat.

 

Nakalimutan ako.

 

 

Baket ang daya talaga ni kupido?

 

Yung mga taong gustong mainlove, hindi niya pinapana.

 

Yung mga taong ayaw mainlove, pinapana.

 

 

Ako, dati. I don't want to fall inlove.

 

Nagdesisyun nako dati na hinding hindi ako magmamahal.

 

Pag nagmahal ka, masasaktan ka. Emotionally. Mentally.

 

Ayos na saken masaktan ng physical. Wag lang mental. Baka masiraan ako ng bait.

 

Pero dati lang yun.

 

 

 

Noong nakilala ko si honeybunch, nagbago lahat.

 

Noong una, natakot parin ako magmahal. Baka masaktan lang ako.

 

Pero nung talagang tinamaan nako ng pana ni kupido, nasabi ko nalang sa sarili ko..

 

"Ang sarap palang magmahal." 

 

 

 

Heaven ang pakiramdam.

 

Idagdag mo pa yung pakiramdam na mahal ka rin ng taong mahal mo.

 

Ang saya lang!

 

 

Pero, sabi nga ..

 

"Hindi habambuhay nasa iyo ang isang bagay. Minsan, kelangan din netong umalis sa piling mo para makita ang totoong siya." 

 

 

Ang sakit lang ng ganun.

 

Baket kelangan pang mawala ng isang bagay para lang makilala ang totoong siya?

 

Hindi ba pwedeng habang nasa piling ko siya, makilala na niya ang totoong siya?

 

 

 

"Dalawa lang ang dahilan kung baket umalis siya sa buhay mo. Either hindi niyo pa oras or hindi talaga siya para sa iyo."

 

 

 

Ang sakit isipin.

 

Buong buhay ko, binigay ko na kay honeybunch.

 

Sa kanya na umiikot yung mundo ko.

 

Siya na nga yata ang mundo ko eh.

 

 

"Wag mo ibigay ang lahat mo para sa isang bagay. Baka mawala ito at hindi na muli mapasaiyo." 

 

 

Baket?

 

Masama bang ibuhos ko lahat ng pagmamahal ko para kay honeybunch?

 

Nagmamahal lang naman ako eh.

 

Wala namang masama pag nagmamahal ah?

 

Sabihin niyo nga.

 

 

 

Mahal na mahal namin ang isa't isa. Pero baket walang happy ending?

 

 

 

 

Love has its own limit.

 

Abuse it, ikaw ang kawawa.

 

Ibigay mo lahat mo, ikaw magdudusa.

 

 

"We might fall for the right person at the wrong time. But love finds its way and seeks the right time for two people to be happy together."

 

 

Honeybunch.

 

I know, you're the one.

 

Wrong time? NO.

 

We loved each other at the right time.

 

 

This is just another chapter of our story.

 

 

 

"To be brave is to love someone unconditionally, without expecting anything in return. To just give. That takes courage; because we don't want to fall on our faces or leave ourselves open to hurt." -Madonna
